     1	using System;
     2	using System.Collections.Generic;
     3	using System.Collections.Immutable;
     4	using System.Globalization;
     5	using System.Linq;
     6	using System.Text;
     7	using System.Threading;
     8	using System.Threading.Tasks;
     9	using Windows.Storage;
    10	using Windows.Storage.Pickers;
    11	using Windows.UI.ViewManagement;
    12	using Tmds.DBus.Protocol;
    13	using Uno.Extensions.Storage.Pickers;
    14	using Uno.Foundation.Logging;
    15	using Uno.UI.Helpers;
    16	using Uno.UI.Helpers.WinUI;
    17	using Uno.WinUI.Runtime.Skia.X11.DBus;
    18	
    19	namespace Uno.WinUI.Runtime.Skia.X11;
    20	
    21	// https://flatpak.github.io/xdg-desktop-portal/docs/doc-org.freedesktop.portal.FileChooser.html
    22	
    23	/// <summary>
    24	/// This class implements v3 of the org.freedesktop.portal.FileChooser portal for files as defined by freedesktop.org.
    25	/// v4 is backwards compatible with v3, so this file also implements v4.
    26	/// </summary>
    27	internal class LinuxFilePickerExtension(IFilePicker picker) : IFileOpenPickerExtension, IFolderPickerExtension
    28	{
    29		private const string Service = "org.freedesktop.portal.Desktop";
    30		private const string ObjectPath = "/org/freedesktop/portal/desktop";
    31		private const string ResultObjectPathPrefix = "/org/freedesktop/portal/desktop/request";
    32	
    33		public async Task<StorageFile?> PickSingleFileAsync(CancellationToken token)
    34			=> await PickFilesAsync(token, false, false)
    35				.ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(StorageFile.GetFileFromPath).FirstOrDefault((StorageFile?)null), token);
    36	
    37		public async Task<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>> PickMultipleFilesAsync(CancellationToken token)
    38			=> await PickFilesAsync(token, true, false)
    39				.ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(StorageFile.GetFileFromPath).ToList(), token);
    40	
    41		public async Task<StorageFolder?> PickSingleFolderAsync(CancellationToken token)
    42			=> await PickFilesAsync(token, false, true)
    43				.ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(path => StorageFolder.GetFolderFromPathAsync(path).GetResults()).FirstOrDefault((StorageFolder?)null), token);
    44	
    45		public async Task<IReadOnlyList<string>> PickFilesAsync(CancellationToken token, bool multiple, bool directory)
    46		{
    47			var sessionsAddressBus = DBusAddress.Session;
    48			if (sessionsAddressBus is null)
    49			{
    50				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    51				{
    52					this.Log().Error($"Can not determine DBus session bus address");
    53				}
    54				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    55			}
    56	
    57			if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    58			{
    59				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    60			}
    61	
    62			using var connection = new DBusConnection(sessionsAddressBus);
    63			var connectionTcs = new TaskCompletionSource();
    64			// ConnectAsync calls ConfigureAwait(false), so we need this TCS dance to make the continuation continue on the UI thread
    65			_ = connection.ConnectAsync().AsTask().ContinueWith(_ => connectionTcs.TrySetResult(), token);
    66			var timeoutTask = Task.Delay(1000, token);
    67			var finishedTask = await Task.WhenAny(connectionTcs.Task, timeoutTask);
    68			if (finishedTask == timeoutTask)
    69			{
    70				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    71				{
    72					this.Log().Error($"Timed out while trying to connect to DBus");
    73				}
    74				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    75			}
    76	
    77			try
    78			{
    79				var desktopService = new DBusService(connection, Service);
    80				var chooser = desktopService.CreateFileChooser(ObjectPath);
    81	
    82				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    83				{
    84					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    85				}
    86	
    87				var version = await chooser.GetVersionAsync();
    88				if (version < 3)
    89				{
    90					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    91					{
    92						this.Log().Error($"File pickers are only implemented for version 3 and above of the File chooser portal, but version {version} was found");
    93					}
    94					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    95				}
    96	
    97				if (!X11Helper.XamlRootHostFromApplicationView(ApplicationView.GetForCurrentViewSafe(), out var host))
    98				{
    99					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   100					{
   101						this.Log().Error($"Unable to get the {nameof(X11XamlRootHost)} instance from the application view.");
   102					}
   103	
   104					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   105				}
   106	
   107				var handleToken = "UnoFileChooser" + Random.Shared.NextInt64();
   108				var requestPath = $"{ResultObjectPathPrefix}/{connection.UniqueName![1..].Replace(".", "_")}/{handleToken}";
   109	
   110				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
   111				{
   112					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   113				}
   114	
   115				// We listen for the signal BEFORE we send the request. The spec API reference
   116				// points out the race condition that could occur otherwise.
   117				var request = desktopService.CreateRequest(requestPath);
   118				var responseTcs = new TaskCompletionSource<(uint Response, Dictionary<string, VariantValue> Results)>();
   119				_ = request.WatchResponseAsync((exception, tuple) =>
   120				{
   121					if (exception is not null)
   122					{
   123						responseTcs.SetException(exception);
   124					}
   125					else
   126					{
   127						responseTcs.SetResult(tuple);
   128					}
   129				});
   130	
   131				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
   132				{
   133					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   134				}
   135	
   136				var actualRequestPath = await chooser.OpenFileAsync(
   137					parentWindow: "x11:" + host.RootX11Window.Window.ToString("X", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
   138					title: (multiple, directory) switch
   139					{
   140						(true, true) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_DIRECTORY_MULTIPLE"),
   141						(true, false) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_FILE_MULTIPLE"),
   142						(false, true) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_DIRECTORY_SINGLE"),
   143						(false, false) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_FILE_SINGLE")
   144					},
   145					options: new Dictionary<string, VariantValue>
   146					{
   147						{ "handle_token", handleToken },
   148						{ "accept_label", string.IsNullOrEmpty(picker.CommitButtonTextInternal) ? ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_ACCEPT_LABEL") : picker.CommitButtonTextInternal },
   149						{ "multiple", multiple },
   150						{ "directory", directory },
   151						{ "filters", GetPortalFilters() },
   152						{ "current_folder", new Array<byte>(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(PickerHelpers.GetInitialDirectory(picker.SuggestedStartLocationInternal)).Append((byte)'\0')) }
   153					});
   154	
   155				if (actualRequestPath != requestPath)
   156				{
   157					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   158					{
   159						this.Log().Error($"{nameof(chooser.OpenFileAsync)} returned a path '{actualRequestPath}' that is different from supplied handle_token -based path '{requestPath}'");
   160					}
   161	
   162					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   163				}
   164	
   165				var (response, results) = await responseTcs.Task;
   166	
   167				if (!Enum.IsDefined((Response)response))
   168				{
   169					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   170					{
   171						this.Log().Error($"FileChooser returned an invalid response number {response}.");
   172					}
   173	
   174					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   175				}
   176	
   177	
   178				if ((Response)response is not Response.Success)
   179				{
   180					if ((Response)response is not Response.UserCancelled && this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   181					{
   182						this.Log().Error($"FileChooser's response indicates an unsuccessful operation {(Response)response}");
   183					}
   184	
   185					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   186				}
   187	
   188				return results["uris"].GetArray<string>().Select(s => new Uri(s).AbsolutePath).ToImmutableList();
   189			}
   190			catch (Exception e)
   191			{
   192				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   193				{
   194					this.Log().Error($"DBus FileChooser error, see https://aka.platform.uno/x11-dbus-troubleshoot for troubleshooting information.", e);
   195				}
   196	
   197				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   198			}
   199		}
   200	
   201		private Array<Struct<string, Array<Struct<uint, string>>>> GetPortalFilters()
   202		{
   203			// Except from the API reference
   204			// filters (a(sa(us)))
   205			//
   206			// List of serialized file filters.
   207			//
   208			// Each item in the array specifies a single filter to offer to the user.
   209			//
   210			// The first string is a user-visible name for the filter. The a(us) specifies a list of filter strings, which can be either a glob-style pattern (indicated by 0) or a MIME type (indicated by 1). Patterns are case-sensitive.
   211			//
   212			// To match different capitalizations of, e.g. '*.ico', use a pattern like: '*.[iI][cC][oO]'.
   213			//
   214			// Example: [('Images', [(0, '*.ico'), (1, 'image/png')]), ('Text', [(0, '*.txt')])]
   215			//
   216			// Note that filters are purely there to aid the user in making a useful selection. The portal may still allow the user to select files that don’t match any filter criteria, and applications must be prepared to handle that.
   217	
   218			// We don't have a way to map a filter to a category (e.g. image/png -> Images), so we make every filter its own category
   219			var list = new Array<Struct<string, Array<Struct<uint, string>>>>();
   220			foreach (var pattern in picker.FileTypeFilterInternal.Distinct())
   221			{
   222				if (pattern is null)
   223				{
   224					continue;
   225				}
   226	
   227				if (pattern == "*")
   228				{
   229					list.Add(Struct.Create("All Files", new Array<Struct<uint, string>>(new[] { Struct.Create((uint)0, "*") })));
   230				}
   231				else if (pattern.StartsWith('.') && pattern[1..] is var ext && ext.All(char.IsLetterOrDigit))
   232				{
   233					list.Add(Struct.Create($"{ext.ToUpperInvariant()} Files", new Array<Struct<uint, string>>(new[] { Struct.Create((uint)0, $"*.{ext}") })));
   234				}
   235				else
   236				{
   237					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   238					{
   239						this.Log().Error($"Skipping invalid file extension filter: '{pattern}'");
   240					}
   241				}
   242			}
   243	
   244			return list;
   245		}
   246	}

```csharp
return results["uris"].GetArray<string>().Select(s => new Uri(s).AbsolutePath).ToImmutableList();
```

When a file path contains spaces, the URI returned by the D-Bus file chooser will encode spaces as `%20`. When you create a `Uri` from this string and then get `AbsolutePath`, it returns the decoded path with actual spaces. However, the issue is that `Uri.AbsolutePath` should properly decode percent-encoded characters.

    10	namespace Uno.UI.Runtime.Skia.MacOS;
    11	
    12	internal class MacOSFileOpenPickerExtension : IFileOpenPickerExtension
    13	{
    14		private static readonly MacOSFileOpenPickerExtension _instance = new();
    15	
    16		private static readonly string[] _asteriskArray = new string[] { "*" };
    17	
    18		private MacOSFileOpenPickerExtension()
    19		{
    20			_filters = Array.Empty<string>();
    21		}
    22	
    23		public static void Register() => ApiExtensibility.Register<FileOpenPicker>(typeof(IFileOpenPickerExtension), _ => _instance);
    24	
    25		// Mapping
    26		// WinUI                            AppKit (NSOpenPanel)
    27		// --------------------------------------------------------------
    28		// CommitButtonText (string)        prompt (NSString)
    29		// ContinuationData (ValueSet)      n/a
    30		// FileTypeFilter                   allowedFileTypes (NSArray)
    31		// SettingsIdentifier (string)      identifier (NSString)
    32		// SuggestedStartLocation (enum)    directoryURL (NSURL)
    33		// User (User)                      n/a
    34		// ViewMode (enum)                  n/a
    35		public void Customize(FileOpenPicker picker)
    36		{
    37			_prompt = picker.CommitButtonText.Length == 0 ? null : picker.CommitButtonText;
    38			_filters = picker.FileTypeFilter.Except(_asteriskArray).Select(ext => ext.TrimStart('.')).ToArray();
    39			_identifier = picker.SettingsIdentifier.Length == 0 ? null : picker.SettingsIdentifier;
    40			_suggestedStartLocation = picker.SuggestedStartLocation;
    41		}
    42	
    43		private string? _prompt;
    44		private string[] _filters;
    45		private string? _identifier;
    46		private PickerLocationId _suggestedStartLocation;
    47	
    48		public async Task<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>> PickMultipleFilesAsync(CancellationToken token)
    49		{
    50			IntPtr array;
    51			if (NativeDispatcher.Main.HasThreadAccess)
    52			{
    53				array = NativeUno.uno_pick_multiple_files(_prompt, _identifier, (int)_suggestedStartLocation, _filters, _filters.Length);
    54			}
    55			else
    56			{
    57				var tcs = new TaskCompletionSource<IntPtr>(TaskCreationOptions.RunContinuationsAsynchronously);
    58				using var registration = token.CanBeCanceled ? token.Register(() => tcs.TrySetCanceled(token)) : default;
    59				NativeDispatcher.Main.Enqueue(() =>
    60				{
    61					if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    62					{
    63						tcs.TrySetCanceled(token);
    64						return;
    65					}
    66					try
    67					{
    68						tcs.TrySetResult(NativeUno.uno_pick_multiple_files(_prompt, _identifier, (int)_suggestedStartLocation, _filters, _filters.Length));
    69					}
    70					catch (Exception ex)
    71					{
    72						tcs.TrySetException(ex);
    73					}
    74				});
    75				array = await tcs.Task;
    76			}
    77	
    78			if (array == IntPtr.Zero)
    79			{
    80				return Array.Empty<StorageFile>();
    81			}
    82	
    83			var files = new List<StorageFile>();
    84			var ptr = Marshal.ReadIntPtr(array);
    85			while (ptr != IntPtr.Zero)
    86			{
    87				var filename = Marshal.PtrToStringUTF8(ptr);
    88				if (filename is not null)
    89				{
    90					files.Add(await StorageFile.GetFileFromPathAsync(filename));
    91				}
    92				array += IntPtr.Size;
    93				ptr = Marshal.ReadIntPtr(array);
    94			}
    95			return files.ToArray();
    96		}
    97	
    98		public async Task<StorageFile?> PickSingleFileAsync(CancellationToken token)
    99		{
   100			string? file;
   101			if (NativeDispatcher.Main.HasThreadAccess)
   102			{
   103				file = NativeUno.uno_pick_single_file(_prompt, _identifier, (int)_suggestedStartLocation, _filters, _filters.Length);
   104			}
   105			else
   106			{
   107				var tcs = new TaskCompletionSource<string?>(TaskCreationOptions.RunContinuationsAsynchronously);
   108				using var registration = token.CanBeCanceled ? token.Register(() => tcs.TrySetCanceled(token)) : default;
   109				NativeDispatcher.Main.Enqueue(() =>
   110				{
   111					if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
   112					{
   113						tcs.TrySetCanceled(token);
   114						return;
   115					}
   116					try
   117					{
   118						tcs.TrySetResult(NativeUno.uno_pick_single_file(_prompt, _identifier, (int)_suggestedStartLocation, _filters, _filters.Length));
   119					}
   120					catch (Exception ex)
   121					{
   122						tcs.TrySetException(ex);
   123					}
   124				});
   125				file = await tcs.Task;
   126			}
   127	
   128			return file is null ? null : await StorageFile.GetFileFromPathAsync(file);
   129		}
   130	}

- `Uri.AbsolutePath` - gets the absolute path of the URI, which is percent-encoded

     1	using System;
     2	using System.Collections.Generic;
     3	using System.Collections.Immutable;
     4	using System.Globalization;
     5	using System.Linq;
     6	using System.Text;
     7	using System.Threading;
     8	using System.Threading.Tasks;
     9	using Windows.Storage;
    10	using Windows.Storage.Pickers;
    11	using Windows.UI.ViewManagement;
    12	using Tmds.DBus.Protocol;
    13	using Uno.Extensions.Storage.Pickers;
    14	using Uno.Foundation.Logging;
    15	using Uno.UI.Helpers;
    16	using Uno.UI.Helpers.WinUI;
    17	using Uno.WinUI.Runtime.Skia.X11.DBus;
    18	
    19	namespace Uno.WinUI.Runtime.Skia.X11;
    20	
    21	// https://flatpak.github.io/xdg-desktop-portal/docs/doc-org.freedesktop.portal.FileChooser.html
    22	
    23	/// <summary>
    24	/// This class implements v3 of the org.freedesktop.portal.FileChooser portal for files as defined by freedesktop.org.
    25	/// v4 is backwards compatible with v3, so this file also implements v4.
    26	/// </summary>
    27	internal class LinuxFilePickerExtension(IFilePicker picker) : IFileOpenPickerExtension, IFolderPickerExtension
    28	{
    29		private const string Service = "org.freedesktop.portal.Desktop";
    30		private const string ObjectPath = "/org/freedesktop/portal/desktop";
    31		private const string ResultObjectPathPrefix = "/org/freedesktop/portal/desktop/request";
    32	
    33		public async Task<StorageFile?> PickSingleFileAsync(CancellationToken token)
    34			=> await PickFilesAsync(token, false, false)
    35				.ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(StorageFile.GetFileFromPath).FirstOrDefault((StorageFile?)null), token);
    36	
    37		public async Task<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>> PickMultipleFilesAsync(CancellationToken token)
    38			=> await PickFilesAsync(token, true, false)
    39				.ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(StorageFile.GetFileFromPath).ToList(), token);
    40	
    41		public async Task<StorageFolder?> PickSingleFolderAsync(CancellationToken token)
    42			=> await PickFilesAsync(token, false, true)
    43				.ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(path => StorageFolder.GetFolderFromPathAsync(path).GetResults()).FirstOrDefault((StorageFolder?)null), token);
    44	
    45		public async Task<IReadOnlyList<string>> PickFilesAsync(CancellationToken token, bool multiple, bool directory)
    46		{
    47			var sessionsAddressBus = DBusAddress.Session;
    48			if (sessionsAddressBus is null)
    49			{
    50				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    51				{
    52					this.Log().Error($"Can not determine DBus session bus address");
    53				}
    54				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    55			}
    56	
    57			if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    58			{
    59				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    60			}
    61	
    62			using var connection = new DBusConnection(sessionsAddressBus);
    63			var connectionTcs = new TaskCompletionSource();
    64			// ConnectAsync calls ConfigureAwait(false), so we need this TCS dance to make the continuation continue on the UI thread
    65			_ = connection.ConnectAsync().AsTask().ContinueWith(_ => connectionTcs.TrySetResult(), token);
    66			var timeoutTask = Task.Delay(1000, token);
    67			var finishedTask = await Task.WhenAny(connectionTcs.Task, timeoutTask);
    68			if (finishedTask == timeoutTask)
    69			{
    70				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    71				{
    72					this.Log().Error($"Timed out while trying to connect to DBus");
    73				}
    74				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    75			}
    76	
    77			try
    78			{
    79				var desktopService = new DBusService(connection, Service);
    80				var chooser = desktopService.CreateFileChooser(ObjectPath);
    81	
    82				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    83				{
    84					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    85				}
    86	
    87				var version = await chooser.GetVersionAsync();
    88				if (version < 3)
    89				{
    90					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    91					{
    92						this.Log().Error($"File pickers are only implemented for version 3 and above of the File chooser portal, but version {version} was found");
    93					}
    94					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
    95				}
    96	
    97				if (!X11Helper.XamlRootHostFromApplicationView(ApplicationView.GetForCurrentViewSafe(), out var host))
    98				{
    99					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   100					{
   101						this.Log().Error($"Unable to get the {nameof(X11XamlRootHost)} instance from the application view.");
   102					}
   103	
   104					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   105				}
   106	
   107				var handleToken = "UnoFileChooser" + Random.Shared.NextInt64();
   108				var requestPath = $"{ResultObjectPathPrefix}/{connection.UniqueName![1..].Replace(".", "_")}/{handleToken}";
   109	
   110				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
   111				{
   112					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   113				}
   114	
   115				// We listen for the signal BEFORE we send the request. The spec API reference
   116				// points out the race condition that could occur otherwise.
   117				var request = desktopService.CreateRequest(requestPath);
   118				var responseTcs = new TaskCompletionSource<(uint Response, Dictionary<string, VariantValue> Results)>();
   119				_ = request.WatchResponseAsync((exception, tuple) =>
   120				{
   121					if (exception is not null)
   122					{
   123						responseTcs.SetException(exception);
   124					}
   125					else
   126					{
   127						responseTcs.SetResult(tuple);
   128					}
   129				});
   130	
   131				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
   132				{
   133					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   134				}
   135	
   136				var actualRequestPath = await chooser.OpenFileAsync(
   137					parentWindow: "x11:" + host.RootX11Window.Window.ToString("X", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
   138					title: (multiple, directory) switch
   139					{
   140						(true, true) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_DIRECTORY_MULTIPLE"),
   141						(true, false) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_FILE_MULTIPLE"),
   142						(false, true) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_DIRECTORY_SINGLE"),
   143						(false, false) => ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE_FILE_SINGLE")
   144					},
   145					options: new Dictionary<string, VariantValue>
   146					{
   147						{ "handle_token", handleToken },
   148						{ "accept_label", string.IsNullOrEmpty(picker.CommitButtonTextInternal) ? ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_ACCEPT_LABEL") : picker.CommitButtonTextInternal },
   149						{ "multiple", multiple },
   150						{ "directory", directory },
   151						{ "filters", GetPortalFilters() },
   152						{ "current_folder", new Array<byte>(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(PickerHelpers.GetInitialDirectory(picker.SuggestedStartLocationInternal)).Append((byte)'\0')) }
   153					});
   154	
   155				if (actualRequestPath != requestPath)
   156				{
   157					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   158					{
   159						this.Log().Error($"{nameof(chooser.OpenFileAsync)} returned a path '{actualRequestPath}' that is different from supplied handle_token -based path '{requestPath}'");
   160					}
   161	
   162					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   163				}
   164	
   165				var (response, results) = await responseTcs.Task;
   166	
   167				if (!Enum.IsDefined((Response)response))
   168				{
   169					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   170					{
   171						this.Log().Error($"FileChooser returned an invalid response number {response}.");
   172					}
   173	
   174					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   175				}
   176	
   177	
   178				if ((Response)response is not Response.Success)
   179				{
   180					if ((Response)response is not Response.UserCancelled && this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   181					{
   182						this.Log().Error($"FileChooser's response indicates an unsuccessful operation {(Response)response}");
   183					}
   184	
   185					return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   186				}
   187	
   188				return results["uris"].GetArray<string>().Select(s => new Uri(s).AbsolutePath).ToImmutableList();
   189			}
   190			catch (Exception e)
   191			{
   192				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   193				{
   194					this.Log().Error($"DBus FileChooser error, see https://aka.platform.uno/x11-dbus-troubleshoot for troubleshooting information.", e);
   195				}
   196	
   197				return ImmutableList<string>.Empty;
   198			}
   199		}
   200	
   201		private Array<Struct<string, Array<Struct<uint, string>>>> GetPortalFilters()
   202		{
   203			// Except from the API reference
   204			// filters (a(sa(us)))
   205			//
   206			// List of serialized file filters.
   207			//
   208			// Each item in the array specifies a single filter to offer to the user.
   209			//
   210			// The first string is a user-visible name for the filter. The a(us) specifies a list of filter strings, which can be either a glob-style pattern (indicated by 0) or a MIME type (indicated by 1). Patterns are case-sensitive.
   211			//
   212			// To match different capitalizations of, e.g. '*.ico', use a pattern like: '*.[iI][cC][oO]'.
   213			//
   214			// Example: [('Images', [(0, '*.ico'), (1, 'image/png')]), ('Text', [(0, '*.txt')])]
   215			//
   216			// Note that filters are purely there to aid the user in making a useful selection. The portal may still allow the user to select files that don’t match any filter criteria, and applications must be prepared to handle that.
   217	
   218			// We don't have a way to map a filter to a category (e.g. image/png -> Images), so we make every filter its own category
   219			var list = new Array<Struct<string, Array<Struct<uint, string>>>>();
   220			foreach (var pattern in picker.FileTypeFilterInternal.Distinct())
   221			{
   222				if (pattern is null)
   223				{
   224					continue;
   225				}
   226	
   227				if (pattern == "*")
   228				{
   229					list.Add(Struct.Create("All Files", new Array<Struct<uint, string>>(new[] { Struct.Create((uint)0, "*") })));
   230				}
   231				else if (pattern.StartsWith('.') && pattern[1..] is var ext && ext.All(char.IsLetterOrDigit))
   232				{
   233					list.Add(Struct.Create($"{ext.ToUpperInvariant()} Files", new Array<Struct<uint, string>>(new[] { Struct.Create((uint)0, $"*.{ext}") })));
   234				}
   235				else
   236				{
   237					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   238					{
   239						this.Log().Error($"Skipping invalid file extension filter: '{pattern}'");
   240					}
   241				}
   242			}
   243	
   244			return list;
   245		}
   246	}

    24	/// v4 is backwards compatible with v3, so this file also implements v4.
    25	/// </summary>
    26	internal class LinuxFileSaverExtension(FileSavePicker picker) : IFileSavePickerExtension
    27	{
    28		private const string Service = "org.freedesktop.portal.Desktop";
    29		private const string ObjectPath = "/org/freedesktop/portal/desktop";
    30		private const string ResultObjectPathPrefix = "/org/freedesktop/portal/desktop/request";
    31	
    32		public async Task<StorageFile?> PickSaveFileAsync(CancellationToken token)
    33		{
    34			var sessionsAddressBus = DBusAddress.Session;
    35			if (sessionsAddressBus is null)
    36			{
    37				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    38				{
    39					this.Log().Error($"Can not determine DBus session bus address");
    40				}
    41				return null;
    42			}
    43	
    44			if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    45			{
    46				return null;
    47			}
    48	
    49			using var connection = new DBusConnection(sessionsAddressBus);
    50			var connectionTcs = new TaskCompletionSource();
    51			// ConnectAsync calls ConfigureAwait(false), so we need this TCS dance to make the continuation continue on the UI thread
    52			_ = connection.ConnectAsync().AsTask().ContinueWith(_ => connectionTcs.TrySetResult(), token);
    53			var timeoutTask = Task.Delay(1000, token);
    54			var finishedTask = await Task.WhenAny(connectionTcs.Task, timeoutTask);
    55			if (finishedTask == timeoutTask)
    56			{
    57				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    58				{
    59					this.Log().Error($"Timed out while trying to connect to DBus");
    60				}
    61				return null;
    62			}
    63	
    64			try
    65			{
    66				var desktopService = new DBusService(connection, Service);
    67				var chooser = desktopService.CreateFileChooser(ObjectPath);
    68	
    69				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    70				{
    71					return null;
    72				}
    73	
    74				var version = await chooser.GetVersionAsync();
    75				if (version < 3)
    76				{
    77					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    78					{
    79						this.Log().Error($"File pickers are only implemented for version 3 and above of the File chooser portal, but version {version} was found");
    80					}
    81					return null;
    82				}
    83	
    84				if (!X11Helper.XamlRootHostFromApplicationView(ApplicationView.GetForCurrentViewSafe(), out var host))
    85				{
    86					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
    87					{
    88						this.Log().Error($"Unable to get the {nameof(X11XamlRootHost)} instance from the application view.");
    89					}
    90	
    91					return null;
    92				}
    93	
    94				var handleToken = "UnoFileChooser" + Random.Shared.NextInt64();
    95				var requestPath = $"{ResultObjectPathPrefix}/{connection.UniqueName![1..].Replace(".", "_")}/{handleToken}";
    96	
    97				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
    98				{
    99					return null;
   100				}
   101	
   102				// We listen for the signal BEFORE we send the request. The spec API reference
   103				// points out the race condition that could occur otherwise.
   104				var request = desktopService.CreateRequest(requestPath);
   105				var responseTcs = new TaskCompletionSource<(uint Response, Dictionary<string, VariantValue> Results)>();
   106				_ = request.WatchResponseAsync((exception, tuple) =>
   107				{
   108					if (exception is not null)
   109					{
   110						responseTcs.SetException(exception);
   111					}
   112					else
   113					{
   114						responseTcs.SetResult(tuple);
   115					}
   116				});
   117	
   118				if (token.IsCancellationRequested)
   119				{
   120					return null;
   121				}
   122	
   123				var actualRequestPath = await chooser.SaveFileAsync(
   124					parentWindow: "x11:" + host.RootX11Window.Window.ToString("X", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),
   125					title: ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_TITLE"),
   126					options: new Dictionary<string, VariantValue>
   127					{
   128						{ "handle_token", handleToken },
   129						{ "accept_label", string.IsNullOrEmpty(picker.CommitButtonText) ? ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_SAVER_ACCEPT_LABEL") : picker.CommitButtonText },
   130						{ "filters", GetPortalFilters(picker.FileTypeChoices) },
   131						{ "current_name", picker.SuggestedFileName },
   132						{ "current_folder", new Array<byte>(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(PickerHelpers.GetInitialDirectory(picker.SuggestedStartLocation)).Append((byte)'\0')) }
   133					});
   134	
   135				if (actualRequestPath != requestPath)
   136				{
   137					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   138					{
   139						this.Log().Error($"{nameof(chooser.OpenFileAsync)} returned a path '{actualRequestPath}' that is different from supplied handle_token -based path '{requestPath}'");
   140					}
   141	
   142					return null;
   143				}
   144	
   145				var (response, results) = await responseTcs.Task;
   146	
   147				if (!Enum.IsDefined((Response)response))
   148				{
   149					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   150					{
   151						this.Log().Error($"FileChooser returned an invalid response number {response}.");
   152					}
   153	
   154					return null;
   155				}
   156	
   157				if ((Response)response is not Response.Success)
   158				{
   159					if ((Response)response is not Response.UserCancelled && this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   160					{
   161						this.Log().Error($"FileChooser's response indicates an unsuccessful operation {(Response)response}");
   162					}
   163	
   164					return null;
   165				}
   166	
   167				return StorageFile.GetFileFromPath(new Uri(results["uris"].GetArray<string>()[0]).AbsolutePath);
   168			}
   169			catch (Exception e)
   170			{
   171				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(LogLevel.Error))
   172				{
   173					this.Log().Error($"DBus FileChooser error, see https://aka.platform.uno/x11-dbus-troubleshoot for troubleshooting information.", e);
   174				}
   175	
   176				return null;
   177			}
   178		}
   179	
   180		private Array<Struct<string, Array<Struct<uint, string>>>> GetPortalFilters(IDictionary<string, IList<string>> filterDictionary)
   181		{
   182			// Except from the API reference
   183			// filters (a(sa(us)))
   184			//
   185			// List of serialized file filters.
   186			//
   187			// Each item in the array specifies a single filter to offer to the user.
   188			//
   189			// The first string is a user-visible name for the filter. The a(us) specifies a list of filter strings, which can be either a glob-style pattern (indicated by 0) or a MIME type (indicated by 1). Patterns are case-sensitive.
   190			//
   191			// To match different capitalizations of, e.g. '*.ico', use a pattern like: '*.[iI][cC][oO]'.
   192			//
   193			// Example: [('Images', [(0, '*.ico'), (1, 'image/png')]), ('Text', [(0, '*.txt')])]
   194			//
   195			// Note that filters are purely there to aid the user in making a useful selection. The portal may still allow the user to select files that don’t match any filter criteria, and applications must be prepared to handle that.
   196	
   197			var list = new Array<Struct<string, Array<Struct<uint, string>>>>();
   198			foreach (var (category, filters) in filterDictionary)
   199			{
   200				var adjustedFilters = filters
   201					.Where(pattern => pattern.StartsWith('.') && pattern[1..] is var ext && ext.All(char.IsLetterOrDigit))
   202					.Select(pattern => Struct.Create((uint)0, $"*{pattern}")); // pattern should be `.extension`. The portal wants a `*.extension` format.
   203				list.Add(Struct.Create(category, new Array<Struct<uint, string>>(adjustedFilters)));
   204			}
   205	
   206			return list;
   207		}
   208	}

    21	
    22	internal class Win32FileFolderPickerExtension(IFilePicker picker) : IFileOpenPickerExtension, IFolderPickerExtension
    23	{
    24		internal const int FilePathBuffer = 1000;
    25	
    26		public Task<StorageFile?> PickSingleFileAsync(CancellationToken token)
    27			=> PickFiles(false, true).ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Count == 0 ? null : task.Result[0], token);
    28	
    29		public Task<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>> PickMultipleFilesAsync(CancellationToken token)
    30			=> PickFiles(false, false);
    31	
    32		public Task<StorageFolder?> PickSingleFolderAsync(CancellationToken token)
    33			=> PickFiles(true, true).ContinueWith(task => task.Result.Select(file => StorageFolder.GetFolderFromPathAsync(file.Path).GetResults()).FirstOrDefault((StorageFolder?)null), token);
    34	
    35		private unsafe Task<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>> PickFiles(bool directory, bool single)
    36		{
    37			using ComScope<IFileOpenDialog> iFileOpenDialog = default;
    38			var fileOpenDialogClsid = CLSID.FileOpenDialog;
    39			var iFileOpenDialogRiid = IFileOpenDialog.IID_Guid;
    40			var hResult = PInvoke.CoCreateInstance(
    41				&fileOpenDialogClsid,
    42				null,
    43				CLSCTX.CLSCTX_ALL,
    44				&iFileOpenDialogRiid,
    45				iFileOpenDialog);
    46	
    47			if (hResult.Failed)
    48			{
    49				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(PInvoke.CoCreateInstance)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
    50				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
    51			}
    52	
    53			hResult = iFileOpenDialog.Value->GetOptions(out var dialogOptions);
    54			if (hResult.Failed)
    55			{
    56				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IFileDialog.GetOptions)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
    57				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
    58			}
    59	
    60			dialogOptions |=
    61				FILEOPENDIALOGOPTIONS.FOS_NOCHANGEDIR
    62				| FILEOPENDIALOGOPTIONS.FOS_FORCEFILESYSTEM
    63				| FILEOPENDIALOGOPTIONS.FOS_FILEMUSTEXIST
    64				| FILEOPENDIALOGOPTIONS.FOS_PATHMUSTEXIST
    65				| (directory ? FILEOPENDIALOGOPTIONS.FOS_PICKFOLDERS : 0)
    66				| (single ? 0 : FILEOPENDIALOGOPTIONS.FOS_ALLOWMULTISELECT);
    67	
    68			hResult = iFileOpenDialog.Value->SetOptions(dialogOptions);
    69			if (hResult.Failed)
    70			{
    71				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IFileDialog.SetOptions)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
    72				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
    73			}
    74	
    75			if (!directory)
    76			{
    77				var fileTypeList = GetFilterString();
    78				using var fileTypeListDisposable =
    79					new DisposableStruct<List<(Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String friendlyName,
    80						Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String pattern)>>(
    81						static list =>
    82						{
    83							foreach (var (name, pattern) in list)
    84							{
    85								name.Dispose();
    86								pattern.Dispose();
    87							}
    88						}, fileTypeList);
    89	
    90				hResult = iFileOpenDialog.Value->SetFileTypes(fileTypeList
    91					.Select(t => new COMDLG_FILTERSPEC { pszName = t.friendlyName, pszSpec = t.pattern })
    92					.ToArray()
    93					.AsSpan());
    94				if (hResult.Failed)
    95				{
    96					this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IFileDialog.SetFileTypes)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
    97					return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
    98				}
    99			}
   100	
   101			using var defaultFolder = SuggestedStartLocationHandler.GetStartLocationShellItem(picker.SuggestedStartLocationInternal);
   102			if (defaultFolder != default)
   103			{
   104				iFileOpenDialog.Value->SetDefaultFolder(defaultFolder);
   105			}
   106	
   107			hResult = iFileOpenDialog.Value->SetOkButtonLabel(string.IsNullOrEmpty(picker.CommitButtonTextInternal) ? ResourceAccessor.GetLocalizedStringResource("FILE_PICKER_ACCEPT_LABEL") : picker.CommitButtonTextInternal);
   108			if (hResult.Failed)
   109			{
   110				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IFileDialog.SetOkButtonLabel)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   111				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
   112			}
   113	
   114			var hwnd = PInvoke.GetActiveWindow();
   115			if (hwnd == IntPtr.Zero)
   116			{
   117				hwnd = Win32WindowWrapper.GetHwnds().First();
   118			}
   119			hResult = iFileOpenDialog.Value->Show(hwnd);
   120			if (hResult.Failed)
   121			{
   122				if (hResult != (uint)WIN32_ERROR.ERROR_CANCELLED)
   123				{
   124					this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IFileDialog.Show)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   125				}
   126				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
   127			}
   128	
   129			using ComScope<IShellItemArray> iShellItemArray = default;
   130			hResult = iFileOpenDialog.Value->GetResults(iShellItemArray);
   131			if (hResult.Failed)
   132			{
   133				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IFileOpenDialog.GetResults)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   134				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
   135			}
   136	
   137			hResult = iShellItemArray.Value->GetCount(out var count);
   138			if (hResult.Failed)
   139			{
   140				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IShellItemArray.GetCount)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   141				return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
   142			}
   143	
   144			var items = new IShellItem*[count];
   145			using var itemsDisposable =
   146				new DisposableStruct<IShellItem*[]>(
   147					static list =>
   148					{
   149						foreach (var ptr in list)
   150						{
   151							if (ptr is null)
   152							{
   153								continue;
   154							}
   155							var hResult = (HRESULT)ptr->Release();
   156							if (hResult.Failed) { typeof(Win32FileFolderPickerExtension).LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IUnknown.Release)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}"); }
   157						}
   158					}, items);
   159	
   160			var ret = new List<StorageFile>();
   161			char* resultName = stackalloc char[FilePathBuffer];
   162			for (var i = 0; i < count; i++)
   163			{
   164				IShellItem* temp = default;
   165				hResult = iShellItemArray.Value->GetItemAt((uint)i, &temp);
   166				if (hResult.Failed)
   167				{
   168					this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IShellItemArray.GetItemAt)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   169					return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>([]);
   170				}
   171				items[i] = temp;
   172	
   173				temp->GetDisplayName(SIGDN.SIGDN_FILESYSPATH, (PWSTR*)&resultName);
   174				if (hResult.Failed)
   175				{
   176					this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IShellItem.GetDisplayName)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   177					continue;
   178				}
   179	
   180				ret.Add(StorageFile.GetFileFromPath(new string(resultName)));
   181			}
   182	
   183			return Task.FromResult<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>>(ret);
   184		}
   185	
   186		private List<(Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String friendlyName, Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String pattern)> GetFilterString()
   187		{
   188			var list = new List<(Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String, Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String)>();
   189	
   190			var hasAnyFilePattern = false;
   191			var wildcardPatterns = new List<string>(picker.FileTypeFilterInternal.Count);
   192			foreach (var pattern in picker.FileTypeFilterInternal.Distinct())
   193			{
   194				if (pattern is null)
   195				{
   196					continue;
   197				}
   198	
   199				if (pattern == "*")
   200				{
   201					hasAnyFilePattern = true;
   202				}
   203				else if (pattern.StartsWith('.') && pattern[1..] is var ext && ext.All(char.IsLetterOrDigit))
   204				{
   205					list.Add((new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String($"{ext.ToUpperInvariant()} files"), new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String($"*.{ext}")));
   206					wildcardPatterns.Add($"*.{ext}");
   207				}
   208				else
   209				{
   210					this.LogError()?.Error($"Skipping invalid file extension filter: '{pattern}'");
   211				}
   212			}
   213	
   214			if (hasAnyFilePattern || list.Count == 0)
   215			{
   216				list.Insert(0, (new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String("All files"), new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String("*")));
   217			}
   218			else if (wildcardPatterns.Count > 1)
   219			{
   220				// If there are multiple patterns, add an "All Files" entry with all patterns merged.
   221				var allPatterns = string.Join(';', wildcardPatterns);
   222				list.Insert(0, (new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String("All files"), new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String(allPatterns)));
   223			}
   224	
   225			return list;
   226		}
   227	}

    13	namespace Uno.Extensions.Storage.Pickers
    14	{
    15		internal class FileOpenPickerExtension : IFileOpenPickerExtension
    16		{
    17			private readonly FileOpenPicker _picker;
    18	
    19			public FileOpenPickerExtension(object owner)
    20			{
    21				if (!(owner is FileOpenPicker picker))
    22				{
    23					throw new InvalidOperationException("Owner of FileOpenPickerExtension must be a FileOpenPicker.");
    24				}
    25				_picker = picker;
    26			}
    27	
    28			public async Task<StorageFile?> PickSingleFileAsync(CancellationToken token)
    29			{
    30				var files = await OpenPickerAsync(false);
    31				return files.FirstOrDefault();
    32			}
    33	
    34			public async Task<IReadOnlyList<StorageFile>> PickMultipleFilesAsync(CancellationToken token)
    35			{
    36				var files = await OpenPickerAsync(true);
    37				return new FilePickerSelectedFilesArray(files);
    38			}
    39	
    40			private async Task<StorageFile[]> OpenPickerAsync(bool multiple)
    41			{
    42				var openFileDialog = new OpenFileDialog
    43				{
    44					Multiselect = multiple
    45				};
    46	
    47				var filterBuilder = new StringBuilder();
    48				var filterIndex = -1;
    49				var fileTypeFilterCount = _picker.FileTypeFilter.Count;
    50				for (var i = 0; i < fileTypeFilterCount; i++)
    51				{
    52					var fileType = _picker.FileTypeFilter[i];
    53					if (fileType == "*")
    54					{
    55						filterBuilder.Append("|All|*");
    56						filterIndex = i + 1;
    57					}
    58					else
    59					{
    60						filterBuilder.Append($"|{fileType}|*{fileType}");
    61					}
    62				}
    63	
    64				if (filterIndex == -1)
    65				{
    66					var fullFilter = string.Join(";", _picker.FileTypeFilter.Select(fileType => $"*{fileType}"));
    67					filterBuilder.Append($"|All|{fullFilter}");
    68					filterIndex = fileTypeFilterCount + 1;
    69				}
    70	
    71				openFileDialog.Filter = filterBuilder.ToString(1, filterBuilder.Length - 1);
    72				openFileDialog.FilterIndex = filterIndex;
    73	
    74				openFileDialog.InitialDirectory = PickerHelpers.GetInitialDirectory(_picker.SuggestedStartLocation);
    75	
    76				var files = new List<StorageFile>();
    77				if (openFileDialog.ShowDialog() == true)
    78				{
    79					foreach (var fileName in openFileDialog.FileNames)
    80					{
    81						files.Add(await StorageFile.GetFileFromPathAsync(fileName));
    82					}
    83				}
    84				return files.ToArray();
    85			}
    86		}
    87	}

   150			{
   151				this.LogError()?.Error($"{nameof(IShellItem.GetDisplayName)} failed: {Win32Helper.GetErrorMessage(hResult)}");
   152				return Task.FromResult<StorageFile?>(null);
   153			}
   154	
   155			var path = new string(resultName);
   156			try
   157			{
   158				// FileSavePicker creates the file if it does not exist yet.
   159				if (!File.Exists(path))
   160				{
   161					File.WriteAllBytes(path, Array.Empty<byte>());
   162				}
   163			}
   164			catch (Exception ex)
   165			{
   166				this.LogError()?.Error($"Could not create file at '{path}'", ex);
   167			}
   168	
   169			var file = StorageFile.GetFileFromPath(path);
   170			return Task.FromResult<StorageFile?>(file);
   171		}
   172	
   173		private List<(Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String friendlyName, Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String pattern)> GetFilterString()
   174		{
   175			var ret = new List<(Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String friendlyName, Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String pattern)>();
   176			foreach (var entry in picker.FileTypeChoices)
   177			{
   178				List<string> patternList = new();
   179	
   180				foreach (var pattern in entry.Value)
   181				{
   182					if (pattern.StartsWith('.') && pattern[1..] is var ext && ext.All(char.IsLetterOrDigit))
   183					{
   184						patternList.Add($"*{pattern}");
   185					}
   186					else
   187					{
   188						this.LogError()?.Error($"Skipping invalid file extension pattern '{pattern}' for key {entry.Key}");
   189					}
   190				}
   191	
   192				ret.Add((new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String(entry.Key), new Win32Helper.NativeNulTerminatedUtf16String(string.Join(";", patternList))));
   193			}
   194	
   195			return ret;
   196		}
   197	}

   190			//

   195			// Note that filters are purely there to aid the user in making a useful selection. The portal may still allow the user to select files that don’t match any filter criteria, and applications must be prepared to handle that.
   196

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Collections.Immutable;
using System.Linq;

class Program
{
    static void Main()
    {
        // Simulate what the old code does
        var testUris = new[] {
            "file:///home/user/my%20file.txt",
            "file:///home/user/Downloads/file%20name%20with%20spaces.pdf",
            "file:///tmp/test%20space.txt",
            "file:///home/user/normal.txt",
            "file:///home/user/100%25%20real.txt"  // %25 is %, then %20 is space
        };
        
        Console.WriteLine("=== Old behavior (AbsolutePath) ===");
        foreach (var uriStr in testUris)
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"Input: {uriStr}");
            Console.WriteLine($"  AbsolutePath: {new Uri(uriStr).AbsolutePath}");
            Console.WriteLine();
        }
        
        Console.WriteLine("=== New behavior (LocalPath) ===");
        foreach (var uriStr in testUris)
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"Input: {uriStr}");
            Console.WriteLine($"  LocalPath: {new Uri(uriStr).LocalPath}");
            Console.WriteLine();
        }
        
        // Simulate what the code does
        var results = new Dictionary<string, string[]>();
        results["uris"] = testUris;
        
        Console.WriteLine("=== Simulating old code ===");
        var oldResult = results["uris"].Select(s => new Uri(s).AbsolutePath).ToImmutableList();
        foreach (var r in oldResult)
            Console.WriteLine($"  -> '{r}'");
            
        Console.WriteLine();
        Console.WriteLine("=== Simulating new code ===");
        var newResult = results["uris"].Select(s => new Uri(s).LocalPath).ToImmutableList();
        foreach (var r in newResult)
            Console.WriteLine($"  -> '{r}'");
    }
}

- **Old behavior** (`AbsolutePath`): Returns paths with `%20` encoding still in place, which would cause the file system to fail to find the file (since the actual path has spaces, not `%20`).
- **New behavior** (`LocalPath`): Properly decodes the percent-encoded characters, returning the actual file system paths.

This confirms that:
1. The issue is real - `AbsolutePath` keeps `%20` (and other percent-encoded characters) in the path
2. `LocalPath` properly decodes them to actual spaces and other characters
3. The fix handles edge cases like multiple encoded characters (`%20`), mixed encoding (`%25` for `%` followed by `%20` for space), and normal paths without encoding
